 Many adopt good habits, but do you know that some bad habits also help us to stay healthy
 kai baar aisa hota he ki jin aadaton ko ham bura samajhakar chhod dete hai, darasal, wo hamaare liye acchhee hoti hai
 These are 5 such habits which we consider to be bad but leave it wrong
 1
 Full cream milk Peenakya You are also among those who go to the shop and ask for toned or double toned milk
 agar aap aisa karte hai to turant apni is aadat ko badal daaliye

 2
 Most of the people who visit on an off day feel that after working for a week, they should only rest on the off day
 lekin aisa sochna or aisa karnaa galat he
 According to a study, it is better to hang out at home than on a day off
 isse shanti milti he

 aaraam karnaa jaruri he lekin ghoomane-phirane ko bekaar samajhnaa galat
 3
 gandagi se rahanaa, itnaa bura bhi nahioti to har cheez kii buree hi hoti he
 If you live very cleanly and think that by doing this you will never get sick, then tell you that your thinking is wrong
 bahut zyada safai se rahane waalon kaa immune system kamajorho jaataa he

 darasal, hamaari twachaa par kai aise bacteria maujuud hote hai jo sehat ke liye achche hote hai

 4

 5
 So how much coffee do you drink? You must have heard many people say that drinking tea and coffee is dangerous for health
